<h1 class="firstHeading mw-first-heading" id="firstHeading"><span class="mw-page-title-main">集合 (数学)</span></h1>
<div class="vector-body" id="bodyContent">
<div class="noprint" id="siteSub">维基百科，自由的百科全书</div>
<div id="contentSub"></div>
<div id="contentSub2"></div>
<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">跳到导航</a>
<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">跳到搜索</a>
<div class="mw-body-content mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="zh"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="noteTA" id="noteTA-307af9e9"><div class="noteTA-group"><div data-noteta-group="Math" data-noteta-group-source="module"></div></div></div><div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:%E6%B6%88%E6%AD%A7%E4%B9%89" title="Wikipedia:消歧义"><img alt="Disambig gray.svg" data-file-height="168" data-file-width="220" decoding="async" height="19" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Disambig_gray.svg/25px-Disambig_gray.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Disambig_gray.svg/38px-Disambig_gray.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Disambig_gray.svg/50px-Disambig_gray.svg.png 2x" width="25"/></a>  此条目介绍的是数学家们所称的“直观”或“朴素”的集合理论。关于更详细的说明，请见「<b><a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%B4%E7%B4%A0%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88%E8%AE%BA" title="朴素集合论">朴素集合论</a></b>」。关于有关集合的现代严格<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%AC%E7%90%86%E7%B3%BB%E7%BB%9F" title="公理系统">公理化</a>理论，请见「<b><a href="/wiki/%E5%85%AC%E7%90%86%E5%8C%96%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88%E8%AE%BA" title="公理化集合论">公理化集合论</a></b>」。</div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Example_of_a_set.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="400" data-file-width="450" decoding="async" height="196" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/Example_of_a_set.svg/220px-Example_of_a_set.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/Example_of_a_set.svg/330px-Example_of_a_set.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/Example_of_a_set.svg/440px-Example_of_a_set.svg.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Example_of_a_set.svg" title="放大"></a></div>一个包含一些<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%9A%E8%BE%B9%E5%BD%A2" title="多边形">多边形</a>的集合</div></div></div>
<p><b>集合</b>（英语：<span lang="en">Set</span>），简称<b>集</b>，是一个基本的<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6%E6%A8%A1%E5%9E%8B" title="数学模型">数学模型</a>，指具有某种特定性质的事物的总体。集合里的事物称作<b><a href="/wiki/%E5%85%83%E7%B4%A0_(%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8)" title="元素 (数学)">元素</a></b>，它们可以是任何类型的<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6%E5%AF%B9%E8%B1%A1" title="数学对象">数学对象</a>：数字、符号、变量、空间中的点、线、面，甚至是其他集合。若<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/87f9e315fd7e2ba406057a97300593c4802b53e4" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.33ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>是集合<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的元素，记作<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x\in A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>∈<!-- ∈ --></mo>
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x\in A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="x\in A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/27bcc9b2afb295d4234bc294860cd0c63bcad2ca" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.913ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>。
</p><p>集合在现代<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6" title="数学">数学</a>无处不在，其基本理论是于<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8D%81%E4%B9%9D%E4%B8%96%E7%B4%80" title="十九世纪">十九世纪</a>末创立的。自20世纪上半叶以来，集合理论，更确切地说是<a href="/wiki/%E7%AD%96%E6%A2%85%E6%B4%9B-%E5%BC%97%E5%85%B0%E5%85%8B%E5%B0%94%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88%E8%AE%BA" title="策梅洛-弗兰克尔集合论">策梅洛-弗兰克尔集合论</a>，一直是为所有数学分支奠定严格实际基础的标准。
</p>

<h2><span id=".E5.AF.BC.E8.A8.80"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="导言">导言</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="编辑章节：导言">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E5.AE.9A.E4.B9.89"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="定义">定义</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="编辑章节：定义">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>简单来说，所谓的一个<i>集合</i>，就是将数个对象归类而分成为一个或数个形态各异的大小整体。
一般来讲，集合是具有某种特性的事物的整体，或是一些确认对象的汇集。构成集合的事物或对象称作“<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%83%E7%B4%A0_(%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8)" title="元素 (数学)">元素</a>”或“成员”。集合的元素可以是任何事物，可以是人，可以是物，也可以是字母或数字等。
</p><p>在数学交流当中为了方便，集合会有一些别名。比如：
</p>
<ul><li>族、系　通常指它的元素也是一些集合。</li></ul>
<h3><span id=".E7.AC.A6.E5.8F.B7"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="符号">符号</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="编辑章节：符号">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>元素通常用<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a,\ b,\ c,\ d,\ x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mtext> </mtext>
<mi>b</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mtext> </mtext>
<mi>c</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mtext> </mtext>
<mi>d</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mtext> </mtext>
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a,\ b,\ c,\ d,\ x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a,\ b,\ c,\ d,\ x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c1be579641768d843a3d598fef227f799d8e2b9d" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:12.238ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>等小写字母来表示；而集合通常用<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbf {A,\ B,\ C,\ D,\ X} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<mo mathvariant="bold">,</mo>
<mtext mathvariant="bold"> </mtext>
<mi mathvariant="bold">B</mi>
<mo mathvariant="bold">,</mo>
<mtext mathvariant="bold"> </mtext>
<mi mathvariant="bold">C</mi>
<mo mathvariant="bold">,</mo>
<mtext mathvariant="bold"> </mtext>
<mi mathvariant="bold">D</mi>
<mo mathvariant="bold">,</mo>
<mtext mathvariant="bold"> </mtext>
<mi mathvariant="bold">X</mi>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbf {A,\ B,\ C,\ D,\ X} }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\mathbf{A,\ B,\ C,\ D,\ X}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/5299e84dd583ec181aad15b7d6d8f16072c45b1d" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:16.76ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>等大写字母来表示。
</p><p>当元素<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</mstyle>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>属于集合<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbf {A} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbf {A} }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\mathbf{A}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0795cc96c75d81520a120482662b90f024c9a1a1" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.019ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>时，记作<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a\in \mathbf {A} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a\in \mathbf {A} }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a\in\mathbf{A}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/203aa487e81d0fca30c297539b6d5ca76f516c7c" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.09ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>。
</p><p>当元素<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<semantics>

<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="bold">A</mi>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbf {A} }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\mathbf{A}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0795cc96c75d81520a120482662b90f024c9a1a1" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.019ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>时，记作<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a\not \in \mathbf {A} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</p><p>如果<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbf {A,\ B} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

<mtext mathvariant="bold"> </mtext>
<mi mathvariant="bold">B</mi>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbf {A,\ B} }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\mathbf{A ,\ B}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c4258940f10fea9dc4b665c5aa70f39e629e49a3" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:5.63ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>两个集合所包含的元素完全一样，则二者相等，写作<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbf {A=B} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

<mo mathvariant="bold">=</mo>
<mi mathvariant="bold">B</mi>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbf {A=B} }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\mathbf{A = B}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d3741c5810eec16fdf64cde6256aee4366f9c1d7" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:7.288ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>
</p>
<h3><span id=".E9.9B.86.E5.90.88.E7.9A.84.E7.89.B9.E6.80.A7"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="集合的特性">集合的特性</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="编辑章节：集合的特性">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b>无序性</b>：一个集合中，每个元素的地位都是相同的，元素之间是无序的。
</p>
<ul><li>集合上可以定义序关系，定义了序关系后，元素之间就可以按照序关系排序。但就集合本身的特性而言，元素之间没有必然的序。（参见<a href="/wiki/%E5%BA%8F%E7%90%86%E8%AE%BA" title="序理论">序理论</a>）</li></ul>
<p><b>互异性</b>：一个集合中，任何两个元素都认为是不相同的，即每个元素只能出现一次。
</p>
<ul><li>有时需要对同一元素出现多次的情形进行刻画，可以使用<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%9A%E9%87%8D%E9%9B%86" title="多重集">多重集</a>，其中的元素允许出现多次。</li></ul>
<p><b>确定性</b>：给定一个集合，任给一个元素，该元素或者属于或者不属于该集合，二者必居其一，不允许有模棱两可的情况出现。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E9.9B.86.E5.90.88.E7.9A.84.E8.A1.A8.E7.A4.BA"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="集合的表示">集合的表示</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="编辑章节：集合的表示">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>集合可以用文字或数学符号描述，称为<b>描述法</b>，比如：</li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A=}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A=}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A=}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/8af9c8f62b6dd59911491b509a8705bc862c4429" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:4.196ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>大于零的前三个<a href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E7%84%B6%E6%95%B0" title="自然数">自然数</a></dd>
<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B=}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>B</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B=}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle B=}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3500d05a8f761313103968e3942c4ed235f88135" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:4.217ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>光的三原色和白色</dd></dl>
<ul><li>集合的另一种表示方法是在大括号中列出其元素，称为<b>列举法</b>，比如：</li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle C=\left\{1,2,3\right\}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

<mo>=</mo>
<mrow>
<mo>{</mo>
<mrow>
<mn>1</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>2</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>3</mn>
</mrow>
<mo>}</mo>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle C=\left\{1,2,3\right\}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle C=\left\{1,2,3\right\}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7ae2729727df777eece6844bb84b36d97219b364" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:12.745ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span></dd>
<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle D=\{}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="," aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b8fa4cba3a446de313920e16251756e27312b825" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:0.647ex; height:1.176ex;"/></span>绿色<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle ,}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>,</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle ,}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="," aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b8fa4cba3a446de313920e16251756e27312b825" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:0.647ex; height:1.176ex;"/></span>白色<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo fence="false" stretchy="false">}</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2cf208e5d370391e66767f13641bd5ee6ad93825" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:1.162ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>尽管两个集合有不同的表示，它们仍可能是相同的。比如：上述集合中，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A=C}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>C</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A=C}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A=C}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ed52cca6b1d39e8eb61d7a419b5b2e11d31056d6" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.608ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>而<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B=D}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>B</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>D</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B=D}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle B=D}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d01ffbeb171c46d20e64d702c00cf10bcc04528c" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.787ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，因为它们正好有相同的元素。
</p><p>元素列出的顺序不同，或者元素列表中有重复，都没有关系。比如：这三个集合<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \left\{2,4\right\}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow>
<mo>{</mo>
<mrow>
<mn>2</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>4</mn>
</mrow>
<mo>}</mo>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \left\{2,4\right\}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \left\{2,4\right\}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b9442e4dd1013e31ec2120017e6254aca55b0ba5" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:5.684ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \left\{4,2\right\}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow>
<mo>{</mo>
<mrow>
<mn>4</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
<mo>}</mo>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \left\{4,2\right\}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \left\{4,2\right\}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/abbfa53b7a15d6d65f9f3d810948a7390ff06168" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:5.684ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>和<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \left\{2,2,4,2\right\}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow>
<mo>{</mo>
<mrow>
<mn>2</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>2</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>4</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
<mo>}</mo>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \left\{2,2,4,2\right\}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \left\{2,2,4,2\right\}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2c052ec44c7271e73553f756e665140ee689fdce" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:10.077ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>是相同的，同样因为它们有相同的元素。
</p>
<ul><li>集合在不严格的意义下也可以通过草图来表示，更多信息，请见<a href="/wiki/%E6%96%87%E6%B0%8F%E5%9B%BE" title="文氏图">文氏图</a>。</li></ul>
<h2><span id=".E9.9B.86.E5.90.88.E9.97.B4.E7.9A.84.E5.85.B3.E7.B3.BB"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="集合间的关系">集合间的关系</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="编辑章节：集合间的关系">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E5.AD.90.E9.9B.86.E4.B8.8E.E5.8C.85.E5.90.AB.E5.85.B3.E7.B3.BB"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="子集与包含关系">子集与包含关系</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="编辑章节：子集与包含关系">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E5%AD%90%E9%9B%86" title="子集">子集</a></div><div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Venn_A_subset_B.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="155" data-file-width="155" decoding="async" height="220" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Venn_A_subset_B.svg/220px-Venn_A_subset_B.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Venn_A_subset_B.svg/330px-Venn_A_subset_B.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Venn_A_subset_B.svg/440px-Venn_A_subset_B.svg.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Venn_A_subset_B.svg" title="放大"></a></div><div class="center" style="width:auto; margin-left:auto; margin-right:auto;">B的子集A</div></div></div></div>
<h4><span id=".E5.AE.9A.E4.B9.89_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="定义_2">定义</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="编辑章节：定义">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>集合<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</semantics>

<semantics>

<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="B" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/47136aad860d145f75f3eed3022df827cee94d7a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的<b>真子集</b>，亦称<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span><b>真包含于</b><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="B" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/47136aad860d145f75f3eed3022df827cee94d7a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，或<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="B" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/47136aad860d145f75f3eed3022df827cee94d7a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span><b>真包含</b><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，记作<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A\subsetneqq B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>⫋<!-- ⫋ --></mo>
<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A\subsetneqq B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A\subsetneqq B}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/76b5046c0f318612eb9edecaa531d6360fea5c9e" style="vertical-align: -1.171ex; width:6.606ex; height:3.176ex;"/></span>或<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B\supsetneqq A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>B</mi>
<mo>⫌<!-- ⫌ --></mo>
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B\supsetneqq A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle B\supsetneqq A}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ddf40bf522816cc5d343735604817625b45363ad" style="vertical-align: -1.171ex; width:6.606ex; height:3.176ex;"/></span>（有时也记作<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A\subset B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A\subset B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A\subset B" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/010e98bb4c817357e3ef7e8fa7fbe2385b2aec6e" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.606ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>或<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B\supset A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B\supset A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle B\supset A}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/450398271587fcd521f7313ee3ebfdb5023e1c07" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.606ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>）。
</p>
<h4><span id=".E5.9F.BA.E6.9C.AC.E6.80.A7.E8.B4.A8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="基本性质">基本性质</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="编辑章节：基本性质">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li>包含关系“<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \subseteq }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>⊆<!-- ⊆ --></mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \subseteq }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\subseteq" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a924f8dcb2847bb8871edfdbf4c6b5cca0669228" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:1.808ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>”是集合间的一个<b><a href="/wiki/%E5%81%8F%E5%BA%8F%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB#非严格偏序，自反偏序" title="偏序关系">非严格偏序关系</a></b>，因为它有如下性质：
<ul><li><b>自反性</b>：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \forall }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi mathvariant="normal">∀<!-- ∀ --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \forall }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\forall " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bfc1a1a9c4c0f8d5df989c98aa2773ed657c5937" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.293ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>集合<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle S}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>S</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle S}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="S" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4611d85173cd3b508e67077d4a1252c9c05abca2" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.499ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle S\subseteq S}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>S</mi>
<mo>⊆<!-- ⊆ --></mo>
<mi>S</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle S\subseteq S}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle S\subseteq S}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ea6649e2e7bc36db669f11251126d6976d7fbb3e" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:6.097ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>；（任何集合都是其本身的子集）</li>
<li><b>反对称性</b>：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A\subseteq B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>⊆<!-- ⊆ --></mo>
<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A\subseteq B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A\subseteq B}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b09068bd2f7ba899aeb883ebe670b2ad07b0c851" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:6.606ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>且<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B\subseteq A\Leftrightarrow A=B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>B</mi>
<mo>⊆<!-- ⊆ --></mo>
<mi>A</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">⇔<!-- ⇔ --></mo>
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B\subseteq A\Leftrightarrow A=B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle B\subseteq A\Leftrightarrow A=B}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9e4391ba38cf37db3c54667130ba8d016aca0c53" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:16.825ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>；（这是证明两集合相等的常用手段之一）</li>
<li><b>传递性</b>：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A\subseteq B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>⊆<!-- ⊆ --></mo>
<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A\subseteq B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A\subseteq B}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b09068bd2f7ba899aeb883ebe670b2ad07b0c851" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:6.606ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>且<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B\subseteq C\Rightarrow A\subseteq C}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>B</mi>
<mo>⊆<!-- ⊆ --></mo>
<mi>C</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">⇒<!-- ⇒ --></mo>
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>⊆<!-- ⊆ --></mo>
<mi>C</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B\subseteq C\Rightarrow A\subseteq C}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle B\subseteq C\Rightarrow A\subseteq C}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/082ea95051f509bbe875a12c2aaae3102a37eeb5" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:16.851ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>；</li></ul></li>
<li>真包含关系“<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \subsetneqq }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>⫋<!-- ⫋ --></mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \subsetneqq }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \subsetneqq }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/59b1428bbc8b9aba770fbe531003a669d798b13a" style="vertical-align: -1.171ex; width:1.808ex; height:3.176ex;"/></span>”是集合间的一个<b><a href="/wiki/%E5%81%8F%E5%BA%8F%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB#严格偏序，反自反偏序" title="偏序关系">严格偏序关系</a></b>，因为它有如下性质：
<ul><li><b>反自反性</b>：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \forall }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi mathvariant="normal">∀<!-- ∀ --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \forall }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\forall " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bfc1a1a9c4c0f8d5df989c98aa2773ed657c5937" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.293ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>集合<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle S}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>S</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle S}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="S" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4611d85173cd3b508e67077d4a1252c9c05abca2" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.499ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle S\subsetneqq S}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>S</mi>
<mo>⫋<!-- ⫋ --></mo>
<mi>S</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle S\subsetneqq S}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle S\subsetneqq S}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4c24aeef14a1729ef66c9724de8002b789e73c07" style="vertical-align: -1.171ex; width:6.097ex; height:3.176ex;"/></span>都不成立；</li>
<li><b>非对称性</b>：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A\subsetneqq B\Rightarrow B\subsetneqq A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>⫋<!-- ⫋ --></mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">⇒<!-- ⇒ --></mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo>⫋<!-- ⫋ --></mo>
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A\subsetneqq B\Rightarrow B\subsetneqq A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A\subsetneqq B\Rightarrow B\subsetneqq A}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b0cd5a914254124ba9085ebec7c9075d819d4d15" style="vertical-align: -1.171ex; width:16.825ex; height:3.176ex;"/></span>不成立；反之亦然；</li>
<li><b>传递性</b>：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A\subsetneqq B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>⫋<!-- ⫋ --></mo>
<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A\subsetneqq B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A\subsetneqq B}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/76b5046c0f318612eb9edecaa531d6360fea5c9e" style="vertical-align: -1.171ex; width:6.606ex; height:3.176ex;"/></span>且<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B\subsetneqq C\Rightarrow A\subsetneqq C}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>B</mi>
<mo>⫋<!-- ⫋ --></mo>
<mi>C</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">⇒<!-- ⇒ --></mo>
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>⫋<!-- ⫋ --></mo>
<mi>C</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B\subsetneqq C\Rightarrow A\subsetneqq C}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle B\subsetneqq C\Rightarrow A\subsetneqq C}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6984aff3e07b01b296f16bc06925469a39f545cb" style="vertical-align: -1.171ex; width:16.851ex; height:3.176ex;"/></span>；</li></ul></li>
<li>显然，包含关系，真包含关系定义了集合间的<a href="/wiki/%E5%81%8F%E5%BA%8F%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB" title="偏序关系">偏序关系</a>。而<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \varnothing }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi class="MJX-variant">∅<!-- ∅ --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \varnothing }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\varnothing " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/00595c5e33692e724937fdcc8870496acce1ac74" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.808ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>是这个偏序关系的<b>最小元素</b>，即：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \forall }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi mathvariant="normal">∀<!-- ∀ --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \forall }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\forall " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bfc1a1a9c4c0f8d5df989c98aa2773ed657c5937" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.293ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>集合<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle S}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>S</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle S}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="S" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4611d85173cd3b508e67077d4a1252c9c05abca2" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.499ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \varnothing \subseteq S}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi class="MJX-variant">∅<!-- ∅ --></mi>
<mo>⊆<!-- ⊆ --></mo>
<mi>S</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \varnothing \subseteq S}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \varnothing \subseteq S}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2a851a3998d756bbc4b173726437938f1d541ea7" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:6.406ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>；且若<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle S\neq \varnothing }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>S</mi>
<mo>≠<!-- ≠ --></mo>
<mi class="MJX-variant">∅<!-- ∅ --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle S\neq \varnothing }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle S\neq \varnothing }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b16a4e19ae4c143c619cab08c890e1e8ff20e0f8" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:6.406ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>，则<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \varnothing \subsetneqq S}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi class="MJX-variant">∅<!-- ∅ --></mi>
<mo>⫋<!-- ⫋ --></mo>
<mi>S</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \varnothing \subsetneqq S}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \varnothing \subsetneqq S}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/560acad647fb1b8112554492d239f1fd01ddfd80" style="vertical-align: -1.171ex; width:6.406ex; height:3.176ex;"/></span>，（空集是任何集合的子集，是任何非空集合的真子集）</li></ul>
<h4><span id=".E4.B8.BE.E4.BE.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="举例">举例</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="编辑章节：举例">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd><ul><li>所有男人的集合是所有人的集合的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%9C%9F%E5%AD%90%E9%9B%86" title="真子集">真子集</a>。</li>
<li>所有自然数的集合是所有<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B4%E6%95%B0" title="整数">整数</a>的集合的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%9C%9F%E5%AD%90%E9%9B%86" title="真子集">真子集</a>。</li>
<li><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \left\{1,3\right\}\subsetneqq \left\{1,2,3,4\right\}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</semantics>

<li><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \left\{1,2,3,4\right\}\subseteq \left\{1,2,3,4\right\}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h2><span id=".E9.9B.86.E5.90.88.E7.9A.84.E8.BF.90.E7.AE.97"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="集合的运算">集合的运算</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="编辑章节：集合的运算">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E4.BD.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="并">并</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="编辑章节：并">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%81%AF%E9%9B%86" title="联集">联集</a></div>
<p>两个集合可以相"加"。<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>和<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="B" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/47136aad860d145f75f3eed3022df827cee94d7a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的<b>联集</b>是将<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>和<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="B" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/47136aad860d145f75f3eed3022df827cee94d7a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的元素放到一起构成的新集合。
</p>
<h4><span id=".E5.AE.9A.E4.B9.89_3"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="定义_3">定义</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="编辑章节：定义">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>给定集合<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="B" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/47136aad860d145f75f3eed3022df827cee94d7a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，定义运算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \cup }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>∪<!-- ∪ --></mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \cup }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\cup" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e8ff7d0293ad19b43524a133ae5129f3d71f2040" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.55ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>如下：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A\cup B=\{e|e\in A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>∪<!-- ∪ --></mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mo fence="false" stretchy="false">{</mo>
<mi>e</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
</mrow>
<mi>e</mi>
<mo>∈<!-- ∈ --></mo>
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A\cup B=\{e|e\in A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A\cup B=\{e|e\in A}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/68c2f043757e8ce1a1ec0ed1f5be099514f55afa" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:17.748ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>或<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e\in B\}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>e</mi>
<mo>∈<!-- ∈ --></mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo fence="false" stretchy="false">}</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle e\in B\}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle e\in B\}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/06c8c388b852d80e6bfee63df600b00bf711eb5c" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:6.851ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>。<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A\cup B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>∪<!-- ∪ --></mo>
<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A\cup B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A\cup B}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/cdb575990bcfbcdf616aa6fd76e8b30bf7fd2169" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.09ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>称为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>和<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="B" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/47136aad860d145f75f3eed3022df827cee94d7a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的<b>联集</b>。
</p>

<h4><span id=".E7.A4.BA.E4.BE.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="示例">示例</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="编辑章节：示例">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd><ul><li><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \{1,2\}\cup \{}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h4><span id=".E5.9F.BA.E6.9C.AC.E6.80.A7.E8.B4.A8_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="基本性质_2">基本性质</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="编辑章节：基本性质">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>作为集合间的二元运算，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \cup }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<ul><li><b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BA%A4%E6%8D%A2%E5%BE%8B" title="交换律">交换律</a></b>：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A\cup B=B\cup A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<li><b><a href="/wiki/%E7%BB%93%E5%90%88%E5%BE%8B" title="结合律">结合律</a></b>：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \left(A\cup B\right)\cup C=A\cup \left(B\cup C\right)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h3><span id=".E4.BA.A4"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="交">交</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="编辑章节：交">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%A4%E9%9B%86" title="交集">交集</a></div>
<p>一个新的集合也可以通过两个集合<b>均</b>有的元素来构造。<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>和<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="B" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/47136aad860d145f75f3eed3022df827cee94d7a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的<b>交集</b>，写作<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A\cap B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>∩<!-- ∩ --></mo>
<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A\cap B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A\cap B" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bb27b38cf9eac6060e67b61f66cd9beec5067f81" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.09ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，是既属于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的、又属于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="B" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/47136aad860d145f75f3eed3022df827cee94d7a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的所有元素组成的集合。
</p><p>若<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A\cap B=\varnothing }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>∩<!-- ∩ --></mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi class="MJX-variant">∅<!-- ∅ --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A\cap B=\varnothing }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A\cap B=\varnothing " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/1325e582d7bc7ad1e30dfef4ee67747895af068e" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:10.996ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，则<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>和<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="B" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/47136aad860d145f75f3eed3022df827cee94d7a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>称作<b>不相交</b>。
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Set_intersection.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="500" decoding="async" height="132" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Set_intersection.png/220px-Set_intersection.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Set_intersection.png/330px-Set_intersection.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Set_intersection.png/440px-Set_intersection.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Set_intersection.png" title="放大"></a></div>A 和 B 的交集</div></div></div>
<h4><span id=".E5.AE.9A.E4.B9.89_4"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="定义_4">定义</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="编辑章节：定义">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>给定集合<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>、<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="B" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/47136aad860d145f75f3eed3022df827cee94d7a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，定义运算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \cap }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>∩<!-- ∩ --></mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \cap }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\cap" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9d4e886e6f5a28a33e073fb108440c152ecfe2d3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.55ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>如下：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A\cap B=\{e|e\in A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>∩<!-- ∩ --></mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mo fence="false" stretchy="false">{</mo>

</mrow>
<mi>e</mi>
<mo>∈<!-- ∈ --></mo>
<mi>A</mi>

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A\cap B=\{e|e\in A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A\cap B=\{e|e\in A}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2359876b8912db4092496fb1c61280f70ebd75f4" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:17.748ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>且<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e\in B\}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>e</mi>
<mo>∈<!-- ∈ --></mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo fence="false" stretchy="false">}</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle e\in B\}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle e\in B\}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/06c8c388b852d80e6bfee63df600b00bf711eb5c" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:6.851ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>。<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A\cap B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>∩<!-- ∩ --></mo>
<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A\cap B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A\cap B" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bb27b38cf9eac6060e67b61f66cd9beec5067f81" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.09ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>称为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>和<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

</semantics>

</p>
<h4><span id=".E5.9F.BA.E6.9C.AC.E6.80.A7.E8.B4.A8_3"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="基本性质_3">基本性质</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="编辑章节：基本性质">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>作为集合间的二元运算，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \cap }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>∩<!-- ∩ --></mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \cap }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\cap" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9d4e886e6f5a28a33e073fb108440c152ecfe2d3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.55ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>运算具有以下性质。
</p>
<ul><li><b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BA%A4%E6%8D%A2%E5%BE%8B" title="交换律">交换律</a></b>：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A\cap B=B\cap A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>∩<!-- ∩ --></mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo>∩<!-- ∩ --></mo>
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A\cap B=B\cap A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A\cap B=B\cap A}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c9192707b022c63da4833c865e2ce5c7ced05860" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:15.278ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>；</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/%E7%BB%93%E5%90%88%E5%BE%8B" title="结合律">结合律</a></b>：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (A\cap B)\cap C=A\cap (B\cap C)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>∩<!-- ∩ --></mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>∩<!-- ∩ --></mo>
<mi>C</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>∩<!-- ∩ --></mo>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo>∩<!-- ∩ --></mo>
<mi>C</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle (A\cap B)\cap C=A\cap (B\cap C)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle (A\cap B)\cap C=A\cap (B\cap C)}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/77add316c4030636d9acb5f11a9d651d2a74a8a1" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:27.594ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>；</li>
<li><b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B9%82%E7%AD%89%E5%BE%8B" title="幂等律">幂等律</a></b>：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A\cap A=A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>∩<!-- ∩ --></mo>
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A\cap A=A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A\cap A=A}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b1aed554bbe8370230d848e7d1900dccb87b972e" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:10.91ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>；</li>
<li><b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%A9%BA%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88" title="空集合">空集合</a></b>：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \forall }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \forall }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\forall " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bfc1a1a9c4c0f8d5df989c98aa2773ed657c5937" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.293ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>集合<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A\cap \varnothing =\varnothing }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

<mo>=</mo>

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A\cap \varnothing =\varnothing }</annotation>
