<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi class="MJX-variant">∅<!-- ∅ --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \varnothing }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\varnothing " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/00595c5e33692e724937fdcc8870496acce1ac74" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.808ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \cap }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>∩<!-- ∩ --></mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \cap }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\cap" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9d4e886e6f5a28a33e073fb108440c152ecfe2d3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.55ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>运算的空集合）。</li></ul>
<p>其它性质还有：
</p>
<ul><li><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A\subseteq B\Rightarrow A\cap B=A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>⊆<!-- ⊆ --></mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">⇒<!-- ⇒ --></mo>
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>∩<!-- ∩ --></mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A\subseteq B\Rightarrow A\cap B=A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A\subseteq B\Rightarrow A\cap B=A}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a8848995318bd9ba281fcacd7fb13c26f43120bc" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:21.151ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span></li></ul>
<h4><span id=".E7.A4.BA.E4.BE.8B_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="示例_2">示例</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="编辑章节：示例">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd><ul><li><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \{1,2\}\cap \{}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo fence="false" stretchy="false">{</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>2</mn>
<mo fence="false" stretchy="false">}</mo>
<mo>∩<!-- ∩ --></mo>
<mo fence="false" stretchy="false">{</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>

<h3><span id=".E8.A1.A5.E9.9B.86"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="补集">补集</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="编辑章节：补集">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B7%AE%E9%9B%86" title="差集">差集</a></div>
<p>两个集合也可以相"减"。<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>在<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="B" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/47136aad860d145f75f3eed3022df827cee94d7a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>中的<b>相对补集</b>，国际上通常写作 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B\setminus A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>B</mi>
<mo class="MJX-variant">∖<!-- ∖ --></mo>
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B\setminus A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle B\setminus A}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4f9fc9ff1d2b0248677aed6da1a89025a859476c" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:5.702ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>，中文教材中有时也会写作<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B-A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>B</mi>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B-A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle B-A}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2cad6e00a7c33e826eea086f6fdde72cb4aa9c27" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:6.348ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>。表示属于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="B" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/47136aad860d145f75f3eed3022df827cee94d7a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的、但不属于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的所有元素组成的集合。
</p><p>在特定情况下，所讨论的所有集合是一个给定的<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%A8%E9%9B%86" title="全集">全集</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle U}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>U</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle U}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="U" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/458a728f53b9a0274f059cd695e067c430956025" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.783ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的子集。这样， <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle U-A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>U</mi>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle U-A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle U-A}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/235b042e2802bc0c2c84a6d691d8ee1b7c8aca47" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:6.366ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>称作<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的<b>绝对补集</b>，或简称<b>补集</b>（余集），写作<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A'}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>′</mo>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A'}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A'" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/98a12527148d6ed68adc91d9b419eb4b92d58ef6" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.428ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>或<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \complement _{U}A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mi>∁<!-- ∁ --></mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>U</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \complement _{U}A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \complement _{U}A}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9ab755bfcf0aa2bdb7d7b492815adc632612061f" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:4.398ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>。
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Set_difference.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" decoding="async" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/83/Set_difference.svg/220px-Set_difference.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/83/Set_difference.svg/330px-Set_difference.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/83/Set_difference.svg/440px-Set_difference.svg.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Set_difference.svg" title="放大"></a></div>相对补集 A - B</div></div></div>
<p>补集可以看作两个集合相减，有时也称作<b>差集</b>。
</p>
<h4><span id=".E5.AE.9A.E4.B9.89_5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="定义_5">定义</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="编辑章节：定义">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>给定集合<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="B" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/47136aad860d145f75f3eed3022df827cee94d7a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，定义运算-如下：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A-B=\{e|e\in A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mo fence="false" stretchy="false">{</mo>
<mi>e</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
</mrow>
<mi>e</mi>
<mo>∈<!-- ∈ --></mo>
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A-B=\{e|e\in A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A-B=\{e|e\in A}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/137ef470a0a79e3d549e0fa9cf40179fff829387" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:18.006ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>且<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e\not \in B\}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>e</mi>
<mo>∉</mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo fence="false" stretchy="false">}</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle e\not \in B\}}</annotation>
</semantics>

<h4><span id=".E5.9F.BA.E6.9C.AC.E6.80.A7.E8.B4.A8_4"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="基本性质_4">基本性质</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="编辑章节：基本性质">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

</math></span><img alt="-" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/04bd52ce670743d3b61bec928a7ec9f47309eb36" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:1.808ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>运算的左零元）。</li></ul>

<h3><span id=".E5.B0.8D.E7.A8.B1.E5.B7.AE"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="对称差">对称差</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="编辑章节：对称差">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E5%AF%B9%E7%A7%B0%E5%B7%AE" title="对称差">对称差</a></div>
<h4><span id=".E5.AE.9A.E4.B9.89_6"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="定义_6">定义</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="编辑章节：定义">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>给定集合<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle B}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>B</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="B" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/47136aad860d145f75f3eed3022df827cee94d7a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，定义<b>对称差</b>运算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \vartriangle }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo class="MJX-variant">△<!-- △ --></mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \vartriangle }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \vartriangle }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3e36caa1be30533906553aa85d0dc734d4ea5ba4" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.678ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>如下：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A\vartriangle B=(A-B)\cup (B-A)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo class="MJX-variant">△<!-- △ --></mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>∪<!-- ∪ --></mo>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mi>A</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A\vartriangle B=(A-B)\cup (B-A)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A\vartriangle B=(A-B)\cup (B-A)}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a88ac13ec5e4d653682bea3c0628ca75611dad57" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:28.47ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>。
</p>
<h4><span id=".E5.9F.BA.E6.9C.AC.E6.80.A7.E8.B4.A8_5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="基本性质_5">基本性质</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="编辑章节：基本性质">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>作为集合间的二元运算，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \vartriangle }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo class="MJX-variant">△<!-- △ --></mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \vartriangle }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \vartriangle }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3e36caa1be30533906553aa85d0dc734d4ea5ba4" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.678ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>运算具有如下基本性质：
</p>
<ul><li><b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BA%A4%E6%8D%A2%E5%BE%8B" title="交换律">交换律</a></b>：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A\vartriangle B=B\vartriangle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mo class="MJX-variant">△<!-- △ --></mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo class="MJX-variant">△<!-- △ --></mo>
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A\vartriangle B=B\vartriangle A}</annotation>
</semantics>

<li><b><a href="/wiki/%E7%BB%93%E5%90%88%E5%BE%8B" title="结合律">结合律</a></b>：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (A\vartriangle B)\vartriangle C=A\vartriangle (B\vartriangle C)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mi>B</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo class="MJX-variant">△<!-- △ --></mo>
<mi>C</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>A</mi>

<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo class="MJX-variant">△<!-- △ --></mo>
<mi>C</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>

<li><b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B9%BA%E5%85%83" title="幺元">幺元</a></b>：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \forall }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<semantics>

<h2><span id=".E8.BF.90.E7.AE.97.E6.80.A7.E8.B4.A8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="运算性质">运算性质</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="编辑章节：运算性质">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>集合的运算除了以上情况之外，集合间还具有以下运算性质：

<h2><span id=".E9.9B.86.E5.90.88.E7.9A.84.E5.85.83.E7.B4.A0.E4.B8.AA.E6.95.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="集合的元素个数">集合的元素个数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="编辑章节：集合的元素个数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E5%9F%BA%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="基数 (数学)">基数 (数学)</a></div>
<p>上述每一个集合都有确定的元素个数；比如：集合 <i>A</i> 有三个元素、而集合 <i>B</i> 有四个。一个集合中元素的数目称为该集合的<a href="/wiki/%E5%9F%BA%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="基数 (数学)">基数</a>。<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8%E5%AF%AB%E6%B3%95&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="数学写法（页面不存在）">数学写法</a>有很多种，不同作者及不同书本用不同的写法:  <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \operatorname {Card} (A),\ \#A,\ |A|,\ {\bar {A}},\ {\bar {\bar {A}}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>Card</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>A</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>,</mo>
<mtext> </mtext>
<mi mathvariant="normal">#<!-- # --></mi>
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mtext> </mtext>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
</mrow>
<mi>A</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
</mrow>
<mo>,</mo>
<mtext> </mtext>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mover>
<mi>A</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">¯<!-- ¯ --></mo>
</mover>
</mrow>
</mrow>
<mo>,</mo>
<mtext> </mtext>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mover>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mover>
<mi>A</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">¯<!-- ¯ --></mo>
</mover>
</mrow>
<mo stretchy="false">¯<!-- ¯ --></mo>
</mover>
</mrow>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \operatorname {Card} (A),\ \#A,\ |A|,\ {\bar {A}},\ {\bar {\bar {A}}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \operatorname {Card} (A),\ \#A,\ |A|,\ {\bar {A}},\ {\bar {\bar {A}}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/49d46b6e7d6fe3f30871a84fc9c72fbda11e4873" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:25.322ex; height:3.509ex;"/></span>。
</p><p>集合可以没有元素。这样的集合叫做<b>空集</b>，用 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \{\}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo fence="false" stretchy="false">{</mo>
<mo fence="false" stretchy="false">}</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \{\}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\{\}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3e6f1caa524dfcc90158ad69a51b5f9577fe5f1f" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:2.325ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span> 或符号<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \varnothing }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi class="MJX-variant">∅<!-- ∅ --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \varnothing }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\varnothing " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/00595c5e33692e724937fdcc8870496acce1ac74" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.808ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>表示。比如：集合<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>是2004年所有住在月球上的人，它没有元素，则<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A=\varnothing }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi class="MJX-variant">∅<!-- ∅ --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A=\varnothing }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A=\varnothing }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7673af72c3180bcf0edabf1054f27fcb07d73188" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.65ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>。在数学上，空集非常重要。更多资讯请参阅<a href="/wiki/%E7%A9%BA%E9%9B%86" title="空集">空集</a>。
</p><p>如果集合只含有限个元素，那么这个集合可以称为<b><a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%89%E9%99%90%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88" title="有限集合">有限集合</a></b>。
</p><p>集合也可以有无穷多个元素，这样的集合称为<b><a href="/wiki/%E6%97%A0%E9%99%90%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88" title="无限集合">无限集合</a></b>。比如：自然数集便是无限集合。关于无穷大和集合的大小的其他资讯请见集合的<a href="/wiki/%E5%8A%BF_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="势 (数学)">势</a>。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.85.AC.E7.90.86.E5.8C.96.E9.9B.86.E5.90.88.E8.AE.BA"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="公理化集合论">公理化集合论</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="编辑章节：公理化集合论">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%AC%E7%90%86%E5%8C%96%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88%E8%AE%BA" title="公理化集合论">公理化集合论</a></div>
<p>若把集合看作“符合任意特定性质的一堆东西”，会得出所谓<a href="/wiki/%E7%BD%97%E7%B4%A0%E6%82%96%E8%AE%BA" title="罗素悖论">罗素悖论</a>。为解决<a href="/wiki/%E7%BD%97%E7%B4%A0%E6%82%96%E8%AE%BA" title="罗素悖论">罗素悖论</a>，数学家提出<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%AC%E7%90%86%E5%8C%96%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88%E8%AE%BA" title="公理化集合论">公理化集合论</a>。在公理集合论中，集合是一个不加定义的概念。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E9.A1.9E"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="类">类</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="编辑章节：类">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>在更深层的<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%85%AC%E7%90%86%E5%8C%96%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="公理化数学（页面不存在）">公理化数学</a>中，<b>集合</b>仅仅是一种特殊的<a href="/wiki/%E7%B1%BB_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="类 (数学)"><b>类</b></a>，是“良性类”，是能够成为其它类的元素的类。
</p><p>类区分为两种：一种是可以顺利进行类运算的“<b>良性类</b>”，我们把这种“良性类”称为<b>集合</b>；另一种是要限制运算的“<b>本性类</b>”，对于本性类，类运算并不是都能进行的。
</p><p><b>定义</b> 类A如果满足条件“<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \exists B(A\in B)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi mathvariant="normal">∃<!-- ∃ --></mi>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>∈<!-- ∈ --></mo>
<mi>B</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \exists B(A\in B)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\exists B(A\in B)" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ae8e390470bfe2e6806c3f461c276d7a3f9019fb" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:11.214ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>”，则称类A为一个<b><u>集合</u></b>(简称为<b>集</b>)，记为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \operatorname {Set} (A)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>Set</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>A</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \operatorname {Set} (A)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \operatorname {Set} (A)}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7dcfd08588aa0c4bf95218c83e16c5cb2caa6f8a" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:6.782ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>。否则称为<b>本性类</b>。
</p><p>这说明，一个集合可以作为其它类的元素，但一个本性类却不能成为其它类的元素。因此可以理解为“本性类是最高层次的类”。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.8F.82.E8.A7.81"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="参见">参见</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="编辑章节：参见">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
